\subsection{SF-ltagunco}

\begin{frame}
\frametitle{ttbar}
\fontsize{5}{1}\selectfont
2015:
\begin{figure}
\centering
\begin{subfigure}[b]{0.24\textwidth}
\includegraphics[width=\textwidth]{../sys_pdf/processed_bg_flat/E_3jets_2015/SF_ltag2015_ttbar_ci0000.pdf}

\subsection{jes-RelativeBal}

\begin{frame}
\frametitle{ttbar}
\fontsize{5}{1}\selectfont
2015:
\begin{figure}
\centering
\begin{subfigure}[b]{0.24\textwidth}
\includegraphics[width=\textwidth]{../sys_pdf/processed_bg_flat/E_3jets_2015/jes_RelativeBal_ttbar_ci0000.pdf}
\end{subfigure}
\begin{subfigure}[b]{0.24\textwidth}
\includegraphics[width=\textwidth]{../sys_pdf/processed_bg_flat/M_3jets_2015/jes_RelativeBal_ttbar_ci0000.pdf}
\end{subfigure}
\begin{subfigure}[b]{0.24\textwidth}
\includegraphics[width=\textwidth]{../sys_pdf/processed_bg_flat/E_4jets_2015/jes_RelativeBal_ttbar_ci0000.pdf}
\end{subfigure}
